</tr><tr><td class="sidebar-navbar" style="line-height:1.6"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r78597503"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r79430951">.mw-parser-output .navbar{display:inline;font-weight:normal}.mw-parser-output .navbar-collapse{float:left;text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .navbar-boxtext{word-spacing:0}.mw-parser-output .navbar ul{display:inline-block;white-space:nowrap;line-height:inherit}.mw-parser-output .navbar-brackets::before{margin-right:-0.125em;content:"[ "}.mw-parser-output .navbar-brackets::after{margin-left:-0.125em;content:" ]"}.mw-parser-output .navbar li{word-spacing:-0.125em}.mw-parser-output .navbar a>span,.mw-parser-output .navbar a>abbr{text-decoration:inherit}.mw-parser-output .navbar-mini abbr{font-variant:small-caps;border-bottom:none;text-decoration:none;cursor:inherit}.mw-parser-output .navbar-ct-full{font-size:114%;margin:0 7em}.mw-parser-output .navbar-ct-mini{font-size:114%;margin:0 4em}</style><div class="navbar plainlinks hlist navbar-mini"><ul><li class="nv--&#123;zh-hans:查看;zh-hant:檢視;&#125;-"><a href="/wiki/Template:%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AD%A6" title="Template:微积分学"><abbr title="查看该模板">查</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-讨论"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AD%A6" title="Template talk:微积分学"><abbr title="讨论该模板">论</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-编辑"><a class="external text" href="https://zh.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AD%A6&amp;action=edit"><abbr title="编辑该模板">编</abbr></a></li></ul></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E6%B6%88%E6%AD%A7%E4%B9%89" title="Wikipedia:消歧义"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/25px-Disambig_gray.svg.png" decoding="async" width="25" height="19" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/38px-Disambig_gray.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/50px-Disambig_gray.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="220" data-file-height="168" /></a></span><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r74069148">body:not(.skin-minerva) .mw-parser-output .ifmobile>.mobile{display:none}body.skin-minerva .mw-parser-output .ifmobile>.nomobile{display:inherit;display:initial}</style><span class="ifmobile"><span class="nomobile">&#160;&#160;</span><span class="mobile"></span></span>关于与“<b>极限 (数学)</b>”标题相近或相同的条目页，请见“<b><a href="/wiki/%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90" class="mw-disambig" title="极限">极限</a></b>”。</div>
<p><b>极限</b>（英语：<span lang="en">Limit</span>）是<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90%E5%AD%A6" class="mw-redirect" title="分析学">数学分析</a>或<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86" class="mw-redirect" title="微积分">微积分</a>的重要基础概念，<a href="/wiki/%E8%BF%9E%E7%BB%AD%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="连续函数">连续</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%BC%E6%95%B0" title="导数">导数</a>都是通过极限来作定义。极限分为描述一个<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%8F%E5%88%97" title="序列">序列</a>的下标愈来越大时的趋势（序列极限），或是描述<a href="/wiki/%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="函数">函数</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E5%8F%98%E9%87%8F" class="mw-redirect" title="自变量">自变量</a>接趋近某个值时的函数值的趋势（函数极限）。
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="函数">函数</a>极限可以推广到网中，而<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%88%97" title="数列">数列</a>的极限则与<a href="/wiki/%E8%8C%83%E7%95%B4%E8%AE%BA" title="范畴论">范畴论</a>中的<a href="/wiki/%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E8%8C%83%E7%95%B4%E8%AE%BA)" title="极限 (范畴论)">极限和有向极限</a>密切相关。
</p>
<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc" />
<h2><span id=".E6.A6.82.E5.BF.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="概念">概念</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：概念"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E6.95.B0.E5.88.97.E6.9E.81.E9.99.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="数列极限">数列极限</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：数列极限"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%88%97%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90" title="数列极限">数列极限</a></div>
<p>以数列<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle a_{n}={\frac {1}{n}}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <msub>

          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>n</mi>

        </msub>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

            <mi>n</mi>

  <semantics>

          </mrow>

      </mstyle>
    </mrow>

  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/790f9209748c2dca7ed7b81932c37c02af1dbc31" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.448ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle a_{n}}"></span>越来越接近0，于是可以认为0是这个序列的"极限"。以下的严格定义来自于<a href="/wiki/%E6%9F%AF%E8%A5%BF" class="mw-redirect" title="柯西">柯西</a>：

  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2209f7842feab6054728e8f4c43090c48382f7a9" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:12.793ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \{a_{n}\in \mathbb {R} \}_{n\in \mathbb {N} }}"></span>，若对任意<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \epsilon &gt;0}">

</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="{\displaystyle a}"></span> ，记作 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to \infty }a_{n}=a}">

            <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x221E;<!-- ∞ --></mi>
          </mrow>
        </munder>
        <msub>
          <mi>a</mi>

          </mrow>
        </msub>

        <mi>a</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>

  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b884bfc1b125402e5fabb2219eb6daf465e58900" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:11.436ex; height:3.676ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to \infty }a_{n}=a}"></span> 或 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle a_{n}\rightarrow a}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <msub>
          <mi>a</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>n</mi>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
        <mo stretchy="false">&#x2192;<!-- → --></mo>
        <mi>a</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a_{n}\rightarrow a}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/95096225df1006c18258be3ef1466f839ba576f0" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:7.292ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle a_{n}\rightarrow a}"></span>。这时也称这个数列是<b>收敛的</b>，反之称为<b>发散</b>。可以证明极限是唯一的，也就是
</p><p><div class="mwe-math-element"><div class="mwe-math-mathml-display mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math display="block" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle [\,(a_{n}\to a)\wedge (a_{n}\to a^{\prime })\,]\Rightarrow (a=a^{\prime })}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle [\,(a_{n}\to a)\wedge (a_{n}\to a^{\prime })\,]\Rightarrow (a=a^{\prime })}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></div><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b2729390cf4e44cd387e8ebf1221a83bd734f0b4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-display mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:35.204ex; height:3.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle [\,(a_{n}\to a)\wedge (a_{n}\to a^{\prime })\,]\Rightarrow (a=a^{\prime })}"></div>
</p><p>直观地说，不论把"差距范围" <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \epsilon }">

</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.87.BD.E6.95.B0.E6.9E.81.E9.99.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="函数极限">函数极限</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：函数极限"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8%E6%A5%B5%E9%99%90" title="函数极限">函数极限</a></div>
<p>考虑定义域为 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }">

<p>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle x}">

</p><p>但有时趋近"极限"不会是那个<a href="/wiki/%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8%E5%80%BC" class="mw-redirect" title="函数值">函数值</a>，考虑定义域为 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

        </mrow>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/786849c765da7a84dbc3cce43e96aad58a5868dc" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }"></span> ，对应规则为
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="mwe-math-element"><div class="mwe-math-mathml-display mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math display="block" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle g(x)={\begin{cases}{\dfrac {x}{x^{2}+1}},&amp;x\neq 2\\0,&amp;x=2\end{cases}}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>g</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mrow>
            <mo>{</mo>
            <mtable columnalign="left left" rowspacing=".2em" columnspacing="1em" displaystyle="false">
              <mtr>
                <mtd>
                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                    <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
                      <mfrac>
                        <mi>x</mi>
                        <mrow>
                          <msup>
                            <mi>x</mi>
                            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                              <mn>2</mn>
                            </mrow>
                          </msup>
                          <mo>+</mo>
                          <mn>1</mn>
                        </mrow>
                      </mfrac>
                    </mstyle>
                  </mrow>
                  <mo>,</mo>
                </mtd>
                <mtd>
                  <mi>x</mi>
                  <mo>&#x2260;<!-- ≠ --></mo>
                  <mn>2</mn>
                </mtd>
              </mtr>
              <mtr>
                <mtd>
                  <mn>0</mn>
                  <mo>,</mo>
                </mtd>
                <mtd>
                  <mi>x</mi>
                  <mo>=</mo>
                  <mn>2</mn>
                </mtd>
              </mtr>
            </mtable>
            <mo fence="true" stretchy="true" symmetric="true"></mo>
          </mrow>
        </mrow>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle g(x)={\begin{cases}{\dfrac {x}{x^{2}+1}},&amp;x\neq 2\\0,&amp;x=2\end{cases}}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></div><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/386122ab627a655426185ef781c4896e29e3b973" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-display mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -3.338ex; width:25.761ex; height:7.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle g(x)={\begin{cases}{\dfrac {x}{x^{2}+1}},&amp;x\neq 2\\0,&amp;x=2\end{cases}}}"></div></dd></dl>
<p>的函数，那么当 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle x}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

      </mstyle>
    </mrow>

  </semantics>

  <semantics>

</p><p>有时趋近的点甚至是不在定义域里(也就是无定义)，考虑到<b>算式</b> ( 本质上是一阶逻辑中的<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%80%E9%98%B6%E9%80%BB%E8%BE%91#項" title="一阶逻辑"><b>项</b></a>，所以下面以冒号来代表符号辨识上的定义，而非"数字"意义上的相等 )
</p>

<h4><span id=".E5.AE.9E.E5.87.BD.E6.95.B0.E5.9C.A8.E6.9C.89.E9.99.90.E5.A4.84.E7.9A.84.E6.9E.81.E9.99.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="实函数在有限处的极限">实函数在有限处的极限</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：实函数在有限处的极限"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>若 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle f}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>f</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle f}"></span> 是一个实函数 ( 也就是<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%9A%E4%B9%89%E5%9F%9F" title="定义域">定义域</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E5%80%BC%E5%9F%9F" title="值域">值域</a>都包含于<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0" title="实数">实数系</a> ) ，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle L\in \mathbb {R} }">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>L</mi>
        <mo>&#x2208;<!-- ∈ --></mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi>
        </mrow>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle L\in \mathbb {R} }</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0913a2035a5674d95af33a6c3fb41d2e146dc273" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.102ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle L\in \mathbb {R} }"></span>，那么
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="mwe-math-element"><div class="mwe-math-mathml-display mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math display="block" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \lim _{x\to c}f(x)=L}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <munder>
          <mo movablelimits="true" form="prefix">lim</mo>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>x</mi>
            <mo stretchy="false">&#x2192;<!-- → --></mo>
            <mi>c</mi>
          </mrow>
        </munder>
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>L</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \lim _{x\to c}f(x)=L}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></div><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c3f174c16cc9e61932ecc7eb71b27a4f10a44fc9" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-display mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:12.781ex; height:3.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \lim _{x\to c}f(x)=L}"></div></dd></dl>
<p>用<a href="/wiki/%CE%95-%CE%B4%E8%AF%AD%E8%A8%80" title="Ε-δ语言">ε-δ语言</a>定义为:对所有的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \varepsilon \ &gt;0}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>&#x03B5;<!-- ε --></mi>
        <mtext>&#xA0;</mtext>
        <mo>&gt;</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \varepsilon \ &gt;0}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9c61af7583aa1e454a952bcfb120873b460b0575" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.925ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \varepsilon \ &gt;0}"></span>，都存在 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \delta \ &gt;0}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>&#x03B4;<!-- δ --></mi>
        <mtext>&#xA0;</mtext>
        <mo>&gt;</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \delta \ &gt;0}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/46a5cf1c76bec3924c737a75da7850fe1e2b74f2" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.89ex; height:2.343ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \delta \ &gt;0}"></span> 使得：对任意 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle x\in D_{f}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo>&#x2208;<!-- ∈ --></mo>
        <msub>
          <mi>D</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>f</mi>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x\in D_{f}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3029cdd2f249918d8f7c504343853c821fd480f6" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:7.231ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle x\in D_{f}}"></span> 满足<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle 0&lt;|x-c|&lt;\delta \ }">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo>&lt;</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mi>c</mi>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mo>&lt;</mo>
        <mi>&#x03B4;<!-- δ --></mi>
        <mtext>&#xA0;</mtext>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 0&lt;|x-c|&lt;\delta \ }</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9c9ff0b0ed13bd4389098a64f996930d71107999" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:15.459ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle 0&lt;|x-c|&lt;\delta \ }"></span>时会有<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle |f(x)-L|&lt;\varepsilon \ }">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mi>L</mi>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mo>&lt;</mo>
        <mi>&#x03B5;<!-- ε --></mi>
        <mtext>&#xA0;</mtext>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle |f(x)-L|&lt;\varepsilon \ }</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c2ebcaad1a5c7b00a224e64437843ffd97d6a6fe" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:14.897ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle |f(x)-L|&lt;\varepsilon \ }"></span>。以逻辑符号来表示即为
</p><p><div class="mwe-math-element"><div class="mwe-math-mathml-display mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math display="block" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle (\forall \epsilon &gt;0)(\exists \delta &gt;0)(\forall x\in D_{f})[\,(0&lt;|x-c|&lt;\delta )\Rightarrow (|f(x)-L|&lt;\epsilon )\,]}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x2200;<!-- ∀ --></mi>
        <mi>&#x03F5;<!-- ϵ --></mi>
        <mo>&gt;</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x2203;<!-- ∃ --></mi>
        <mi>&#x03B4;<!-- δ --></mi>
        <mo>&gt;</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x2200;<!-- ∀ --></mi>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo>&#x2208;<!-- ∈ --></mo>
        <msub>
          <mi>D</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>f</mi>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">[</mo>
        <mspace width="thinmathspace" />
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo>&lt;</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mi>c</mi>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mo>&lt;</mo>
        <mi>&#x03B4;<!-- δ --></mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">&#x21D2;<!-- ⇒ --></mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mi>L</mi>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mo>&lt;</mo>
        <mi>&#x03F5;<!-- ϵ --></mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mspace width="thinmathspace" />
        <mo stretchy="false">]</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (\forall \epsilon &gt;0)(\exists \delta &gt;0)(\forall x\in D_{f})[\,(0&lt;|x-c|&lt;\delta )\Rightarrow (|f(x)-L|&lt;\epsilon )\,]}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></div><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2a9217f80f53196f013a83747b3488ab12f5a229" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-display mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:65.407ex; height:3.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle (\forall \epsilon &gt;0)(\exists \delta &gt;0)(\forall x\in D_{f})[\,(0&lt;|x-c|&lt;\delta )\Rightarrow (|f(x)-L|&lt;\epsilon )\,]}"></div>
</p>
<h4><span id=".E5.AE.9E.E5.87.BD.E6.95.B0.E5.9C.A8.E6.97.A0.E7.A9.B7.E8.BF.9C.E5.A4.84.E7.9A.84.E6.9E.81.E9.99.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="实函数在无穷远处的极限">实函数在无穷远处的极限</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：实函数在无穷远处的极限"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>与函数趋于某个给定值时的极限概念相关的是函数在<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E7%A9%B7" title="无穷">无穷</a>远处的概念。这个概念不能从字面上直接理解为：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle x}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>x</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="{\displaystyle x}"></span>距离无穷远越来越小的状态，因为无穷不是一个给定的数，也不能比较距离无穷的远近。因此，我们用<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle x}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>x</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="{\displaystyle x}"></span>越来越大（如果讨论正无穷时）来替代。
</p><p>例如考虑<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)={\frac {2x}{x+1}}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mfrac>
            <mrow>
              <mn>2</mn>
              <mi>x</mi>
            </mrow>
            <mrow>
              <mi>x</mi>
              <mo>+</mo>
              <mn>1</mn>
            </mrow>
          </mfrac>
        </mrow>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)={\frac {2x}{x+1}}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/477d975e65fcfd55718757cdaee5d3c161cd10a8" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:13.685ex; height:5.343ex;" alt="{\displaystyle f(x)={\frac {2x}{x+1}}}"></span>.
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle f(100)=1.9802}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mn>100</mn>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mn>1.9802</mn>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(100)=1.9802}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/be05d344718a5885d80ca1a3ba10d6b053e14927" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:16.133ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle f(100)=1.9802}"></span></dd>
<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle f(1000)=1.9980}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mn>1000</mn>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mn>1.9980</mn>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(1000)=1.9980}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4f7d4e9ca36810c5216d09bcff2f8d7a8dd180d6" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:17.295ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle f(1000)=1.9980}"></span></dd>
<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle f(10000)=1.9998}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mn>10000</mn>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mn>1.9998</mn>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(10000)=1.9998}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/fe0df7c84667099ea6f93b529db1ad1d612a2746" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:18.458ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle f(10000)=1.9998}"></span></dd></dl>
<p>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle x}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>x</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="{\displaystyle x}"></span>非常大的时候，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/202945cce41ecebb6f643f31d119c514bec7a074" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.418ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle f(x)}"></span>的值会趋于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle 2}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mn>2</mn>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 2}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/901fc910c19990d0dbaaefe4726ceb1a4e217a0f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.162ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle 2}"></span>。事实上，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/202945cce41ecebb6f643f31d119c514bec7a074" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.418ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle f(x)}"></span>与<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle 2}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mn>2</mn>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 2}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/901fc910c19990d0dbaaefe4726ceb1a4e217a0f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.162ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle 2}"></span>之间的距离可以变得任意小，只要我们选取一个足够大的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle x}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>x</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="{\displaystyle x}"></span>就可以了。此时，我们称<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/202945cce41ecebb6f643f31d119c514bec7a074" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.418ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle f(x)}"></span>趋向于（正）无穷时的极限是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle 2}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mn>2</mn>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 2}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/901fc910c19990d0dbaaefe4726ceb1a4e217a0f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.162ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle 2}"></span>。可以写为
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="mwe-math-element"><div class="mwe-math-mathml-display mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math display="block" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \lim _{x\to \infty }f(x)=2}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <munder>
          <mo movablelimits="true" form="prefix">lim</mo>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>x</mi>
            <mo stretchy="false">&#x2192;<!-- → --></mo>
            <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x221E;<!-- ∞ --></mi>
          </mrow>
        </munder>
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mn>2</mn>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \lim _{x\to \infty }f(x)=2}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></div><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c3f89ec9b6a74c4f089098a1a2686887804b7e94" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-display mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:13.292ex; height:3.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \lim _{x\to \infty }f(x)=2}"></div></dd></dl>
<p>形式上，我们可以定义：
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="mwe-math-element"><div class="mwe-math-mathml-display mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math display="block" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \lim _{x\to \infty }f(x)=L}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <munder>
          <mo movablelimits="true" form="prefix">lim</mo>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>x</mi>
            <mo stretchy="false">&#x2192;<!-- → --></mo>
            <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x221E;<!-- ∞ --></mi>
          </mrow>
        </munder>
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>L</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \lim _{x\to \infty }f(x)=L}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></div><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/683c0a63b1ce848d887cd4e3db72dcf747227388" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-display mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:13.712ex; height:3.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \lim _{x\to \infty }f(x)=L}"></div></dd></dl>
<p>为
</p><p><div class="mwe-math-element"><div class="mwe-math-mathml-display mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math display="block" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle (\forall \epsilon &gt;0)(\exists \delta &gt;0)(\forall x\in D_{f})[\,(\delta &lt;x)\Rightarrow (|f(x)-L|&lt;\epsilon )\,]}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x2200;<!-- ∀ --></mi>
        <mi>&#x03F5;<!-- ϵ --></mi>
        <mo>&gt;</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x2203;<!-- ∃ --></mi>
        <mi>&#x03B4;<!-- δ --></mi>
        <mo>&gt;</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x2200;<!-- ∀ --></mi>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo>&#x2208;<!-- ∈ --></mo>
        <msub>
          <mi>D</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>f</mi>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">[</mo>
        <mspace width="thinmathspace" />
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>&#x03B4;<!-- δ --></mi>
        <mo>&lt;</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">&#x21D2;<!-- ⇒ --></mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mi>L</mi>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mo>&lt;</mo>
        <mi>&#x03F5;<!-- ϵ --></mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mspace width="thinmathspace" />
        <mo stretchy="false">]</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (\forall \epsilon &gt;0)(\exists \delta &gt;0)(\forall x\in D_{f})[\,(\delta &lt;x)\Rightarrow (|f(x)-L|&lt;\epsilon )\,]}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></div><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/75901e7f2b7f5de658b33c2073ec1fc6f2731a0c" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-display mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:56.005ex; height:3.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle (\forall \epsilon &gt;0)(\exists \delta &gt;0)(\forall x\in D_{f})[\,(\delta &lt;x)\Rightarrow (|f(x)-L|&lt;\epsilon )\,]}"></div>
</p><p>类似地，我们也可以定义：
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="mwe-math-element"><div class="mwe-math-mathml-display mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math display="block" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \lim _{x\to -\infty }f(x)=L}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>x</mi>
            <mo stretchy="false">&#x2192;<!-- → --></mo>
            <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
            <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x221E;<!-- ∞ --></mi>
          </mrow>
        </munder>
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>L</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \lim _{x\to -\infty }f(x)=L}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></div><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c87977d0087d6828de10570e566c35dbe8fdba08" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-display mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:14.991ex; height:4.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \lim _{x\to -\infty }f(x)=L}"></div></dd></dl>
<p>为
</p><p><div class="mwe-math-element"><div class="mwe-math-mathml-display mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math display="block" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle (\forall \epsilon &gt;0)(\exists \delta &lt;0)(\forall x\in D_{f})[\,(x&lt;\delta )\Rightarrow (|f(x)-L|&lt;\epsilon )\,]}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x2200;<!-- ∀ --></mi>
        <mi>&#x03F5;<!-- ϵ --></mi>
        <mo>&gt;</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x2203;<!-- ∃ --></mi>
        <mi>&#x03B4;<!-- δ --></mi>
        <mo>&lt;</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x2200;<!-- ∀ --></mi>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo>&#x2208;<!-- ∈ --></mo>
        <msub>
          <mi>D</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>f</mi>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">[</mo>
        <mspace width="thinmathspace" />

        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo>&lt;</mo>
        <mi>&#x03B4;<!-- δ --></mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">&#x21D2;<!-- ⇒ --></mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mi>L</mi>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mo>&lt;</mo>
        <mi>&#x03F5;<!-- ϵ --></mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mspace width="thinmathspace" />
        <mo stretchy="false">]</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (\forall \epsilon &gt;0)(\exists \delta &lt;0)(\forall x\in D_{f})[\,(x&lt;\delta )\Rightarrow (|f(x)-L|&lt;\epsilon )\,]}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></div><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9286f66165368b3fabd14f14b532df8ffbc4d4ce" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-display mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:56.005ex; height:3.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle (\forall \epsilon &gt;0)(\exists \delta &lt;0)(\forall x\in D_{f})[\,(x&lt;\delta )\Rightarrow (|f(x)-L|&lt;\epsilon )\,]}"></div>
</p>
<h2><span id=".E7.AC.A6.E5.8F.B7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="符号">符号</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：符号"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>极限的符号为lim，它出自拉丁文limit（界限）的前三个字母。
</p><p>在1786年出版的德国人浏伊连（S. L'Huilier）的书中，第一次使用这个符号。不过，“<i>x</i>趋于<i>a</i>”当时都记作“<i>x</i>=<i>a</i>”，直到20世纪人们才逐渐用“→”替代“=”。
</p><p>英国近代数学家<a href="/wiki/%E6%88%88%E5%BC%97%E9%9B%B7%C2%B7%E5%93%88%E7%BD%97%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E5%93%88%E4%BB%A3" title="戈弗雷·哈罗德·哈代">哈代</a>是第一个使用现代极限符号的人。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E6.80.A7.E8.B4.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="性质">性质</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：性质"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to c}S\cdot f(n)=S\cdot \lim _{n\to c}f(n)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <munder>
          <mo movablelimits="true" form="prefix">lim</mo>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>n</mi>
            <mo stretchy="false">&#x2192;<!-- → --></mo>
            <mi>c</mi>
          </mrow>
        </munder>
        <mi>S</mi>
        <mo>&#x22C5;<!-- ⋅ --></mo>
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>n</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>S</mi>
        <mo>&#x22C5;<!-- ⋅ --></mo>
        <munder>
          <mo movablelimits="true" form="prefix">lim</mo>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>n</mi>
            <mo stretchy="false">&#x2192;<!-- → --></mo>
            <mi>c</mi>
          </mrow>
        </munder>
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>n</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to c}S\cdot f(n)=S\cdot \lim _{n\to c}f(n)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/56471a50b30061088ae0fb5f2dcb82dcb96c03aa" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:25.877ex; height:3.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to c}S\cdot f(n)=S\cdot \lim _{n\to c}f(n)}"></span>，这里S是个<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%A7%E7%A9%8D" class="mw-redirect mw-disambig" title="内积">内积</a>算法。</li>
<li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to c}b{f(n)}=b\,{\lim _{n\to c}f(n)}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <munder>
          <mo movablelimits="true" form="prefix">lim</mo>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>n</mi>
            <mo stretchy="false">&#x2192;<!-- → --></mo>
            <mi>c</mi>
          </mrow>
        </munder>
        <mi>b</mi>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mi>f</mi>
          <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
          <mi>n</mi>
          <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>b</mi>
        <mspace width="thinmathspace" />
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <munder>
            <mo movablelimits="true" form="prefix">lim</mo>
            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
              <mi>n</mi>
              <mo stretchy="false">&#x2192;<!-- → --></mo>
              <mi>c</mi>
            </mrow>
          </munder>
          <mi>f</mi>
          <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
          <mi>n</mi>
          <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        </mrow>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to c}b{f(n)}=b\,{\lim _{n\to c}f(n)}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/89737e9de94b82cdc5cae1c50a1499eaea7e5d0c" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:21.903ex; height:3.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to c}b{f(n)}=b\,{\lim _{n\to c}f(n)}}"></span>，这里<i>b</i>是常量。</li></ul>
<p>以下规则只有当等号右边的极限存在并且不为无限时才成立：
</p>
<ul><li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to c}[f(n)+g(n)]=\lim _{n\to c}f(n)+\lim _{n\to c}g(n)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <munder>
          <mo movablelimits="true" form="prefix">lim</mo>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>n</mi>
            <mo stretchy="false">&#x2192;<!-- → --></mo>
            <mi>c</mi>
          </mrow>
        </munder>
        <mo stretchy="false">[</mo>
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>n</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>+</mo>
        <mi>g</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>n</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">]</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <munder>
          <mo movablelimits="true" form="prefix">lim</mo>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>n</mi>
            <mo stretchy="false">&#x2192;<!-- → --></mo>
            <mi>c</mi>
          </mrow>
        </munder>
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>n</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>+</mo>
        <munder>
          <mo movablelimits="true" form="prefix">lim</mo>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>n</mi>
            <mo stretchy="false">&#x2192;<!-- → --></mo>
            <mi>c</mi>
          </mrow>
        </munder>
        <mi>g</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>n</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to c}[f(n)+g(n)]=\lim _{n\to c}f(n)+\lim _{n\to c}g(n)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/93c534ba9bebdbc1a0a473f45dc2ede5194b0a4d" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:38.476ex; height:3.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to c}[f(n)+g(n)]=\lim _{n\to c}f(n)+\lim _{n\to c}g(n)}"></span></li>
<li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to c}[f(n)-g(n)]=\lim _{n\to c}f(n)-\lim _{n\to c}g(n)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <munder>
          <mo movablelimits="true" form="prefix">lim</mo>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>n</mi>
            <mo stretchy="false">&#x2192;<!-- → --></mo>
            <mi>c</mi>

<h2><span id=".E6.8E.A8.E5.B9.BF"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="推广">推广</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：推广"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E6.8B.93.E6.89.91.E7.BD.91"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="拓扑网">拓扑网</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：拓扑网"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E7%B6%B2_(%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8)" title="网 (数学)">网 (数学)</a></div>
<p>在引入<a href="/wiki/%E7%B6%B2_(%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8)" title="网 (数学)">网</a>的概念下，上述的定义可以毫无障碍地推广到任何<a href="/wiki/%E6%8B%93%E6%89%91%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="拓扑空间">拓扑空间</a>。事实上，现代数学中的极限概念就是定义在拓扑空间上的，上述的例子都是拓扑空间的具体化。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.8C.83.E7.95.B4.E8.AE.BA"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="范畴论">范畴论</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：范畴论"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E8%8C%83%E7%95%B4%E8%AE%BA)" title="极限 (范畴论)">极限 (范畴论)</a></div>
<p>范畴论中许多泛性质也可从极限来理解。范畴论极限分为极限与余极限（又称上极限），彼此的定义相对偶。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.A4.96.E9.83.A8.E9.80.A3.E7.B5.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="外部連結">外部链接</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：外部链接"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><span class="citation mathworld" id="Reference-Mathworld-Limit"><cite class="citation web"><a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%83%E9%87%8C%E5%85%8B%C2%B7%E9%9F%A6%E6%96%AF%E5%9D%A6%E5%9B%A0" title="埃里克·韦斯坦因">埃里克·韦斯坦因</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://mathworld.wolfram.com/Limit.html">Limit</a>. <a href="/wiki/MathWorld" title="MathWorld">MathWorld</a>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90+%28%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%29&amp;rft.atitle=Limit&amp;rft.au=%E5%9F%83%E9%87%8C%E5%85%8B%C2%B7%E9%9F%A6%E6%96%AF%E5%9D%A6%E5%9B%A0&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.jtitle=MathWorld&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fmathworld.wolfram.com%2FLimit.html&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal" class="Z3988"><span style="display:none;">&#160;</span></span></span></li>
